|+                     2. Graphical routing                       +|

|++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++|
--------------------------------------------------------------------

1. [-], [num], [.], [>], [<] : Nucleotide
2. [|]                       : Crossover
3. [A], [T], [G], [C]        : Sequence
4. [ a: b], c                : From starting base ID(a) to ending base ID(b), total # of bases (c)
5. [5'], [3']                : Strand direction
